
gsk_akyuu_template = {
    name = "gsk_akyuu_name"
    trait = gsk_akyuu
    age = 16
    gender = female 
    intrigue = { 10 15 }
    martial = { 10 15 }
    diplomacy = { 10 15 }
    stewardship = { 10 15 }
    learning = { 10 15 }
    prowess = { 16 21 }
    trait = brave
    trait = greedy
    trait = forgiving
    trait = education_martial_4
    trait = beauty_good_1
    trait = intellect_good_2
    random_traits = no
    after_creation = {
		dynasty = {
			set_dynasty_name = gsk_dynasty_akyuu_name
		}
		house = {
			set_house_name_from_dynasty = prev.dynasty
		}
        set_touhou_character_sexuality_script= yes
	}
}
